âš™ï¸ Step 3: Backend Setup (Node.js Server)
In /var/www/cyberkeris/server/server.js :
const express = require("express"); const jwt = require("jsonwebtoken");
const bcrypt = require("bcrypt"); const sqlite3 =
require("sqlite3").verbose(); const cors = require("cors"); const app =
express(); const PORT = 3000; const SECRET = "supersecretkey";
app.use(express.json()); app.use(cors());
app.use(express.static("../public")); // Database const db = new
sqlite3.Database("./db/users.db"); db.run("CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS
users (id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY, username TEXT, password TEXT)"); //
Register (optional) app.post("/api/register", async (req, res) => { const
{ username, password } = req.body; const hash = await
bcrypt.hash(password, 10); db.run("INSERT INTO users (username, password)
VALUES (?, ?)", [username, hash]); res.json({ message: "User registered"
}); }); // Login app.post("/api/login", (req, res) => { const { username,
password } = req.body; db.get("SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ?",
[username], async (err, row) => { if (!row) return res.status(401).json({
error: "Invalid credentials" }); const valid = await
bcrypt.compare(password, row.password); if (!valid) return
res.status(401).json({ error: "Invalid credentials" }); const token =
jwt.sign({ username }, SECRET, { expiresIn: "1h" }); res.json({ token });
}); }); app.listen(PORT, () => console.log(`Server running on port
${PORT}`));

require('dotenv').config(); const express = require('express'); const
bodyParser = require('body-parser'); const passport = require('passport');
const GoogleStrategy = require('passport-google-oauth20').Strategy; const
FacebookStrategy = require('passport-facebook').Strategy; const
OAuth2Strategy = require('passport-oauth2').Strategy; // generic OAuth2
for TikTok const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken'); const bcrypt =
require('bcryptjs'); const sqlite3 = require('sqlite3').verbose(); const
cors = require('cors'); const nodemailer = require('nodemailer'); const
app = express(); const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000; const JWT_SECRET =
process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'replace_this_secret'; // === DB init === const
db = new sqlite3.Database('./db/users.db', (err) => { if (err)
console.error('DB:', err); }); db.serialize(() => { db.run(` CREATE TABLE
IF NOT EXISTS users ( id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, email TEXT, name TEXT,
password_hash TEXT, provider TEXT, provider_id TEXT, role TEXT DEFAULT
'client', approved INTEGER DEFAULT 0, created_at DATETIME DEFAULT
CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ) `); }); // === Middleware ===
app.use(bodyParser.json()); app.use(cors());
app.use(passport.initialize()); app.use(express.static('../public')); //
=== Nodemailer transporter (simple) === const transporter =
nodemailer.createTransport({ host: process.env.SMTP_HOST, port:
Number(process.env.SMTP_PORT || 587), secure: process.env.SMTP_SECURE ===
'true', auth: { user: process.env.SMTP_USER, pass: process.env.SMTP_PASS }
}); // helper: send mail async function sendMail(to, subject, text) { if
(!transporter) return; try { await transporter.sendMail({ from:
process.env.SMTP_FROM, to, subject, text }); } catch (e) {
console.error('Mail error', e); } } // === JWT helper === function
issueToken(payload) { return jwt.sign(payload, JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn:
'2h' }); } // === Local email/password signup/login endpoints === const {
v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid'); app.post('/auth/email/signup', async (req,
res) => { const { email, password, name } = req.body; if (!email ||
!password) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'email & password
required' }); const hash = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10); const id =
uuidv4(); db.get('SELECT * FROM users WHERE email = ?', [email], (err,
row) => { if (row) return res.status(409).json({ error: 'User exists' });
db.run( 'INSERT INTO users (id,email,name,password_hash,provider,approved)
VALUES (?,?,?,?,?,0)', [id, email, name || '', hash, 'email'], (err2) => {
if (err2) { console.error(err2); return res.status(500).json({ error: 'db
error' }); } // notify admin sendMail(process.env.ADMIN_EMAIL, 'New signup
pending', `New signup: ${email}`); res.json({ message: 'Signup created,
pending admin approval' }); } ); }); }); app.post('/auth/email/login',
(req, res) => { const { email, password } = req.body; db.get('SELECT *
FROM users WHERE email = ?', [email], async (err, user) => { if (!user)
return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' }); if

7) Security & Deployment notes (must read)
Never commit .env to git. Store secrets in VPS environment or secret manager.
Use a strong JWT_SECRET and ADMIN_KEY .
For production, protect admin endpoints with proper auth (not just an admin key
header). Use RBAC.
TikTok OAuth may require extra steps (TikTok often needs explicit userinfo request
after exchange). Check their docs to implement userinfo call
in /auth/tiktok/callback .
Consider implementing refresh tokens (JWT rotation) for long sessions.
Add rate limiting (e.g., express-rate-limit ) to /auth routes.
Use HTTPS everywhere and HSTS via Cloudflare or Nginx.

whitelist of specific admin addresses (e.g., env var ADMIN_EMAIL_WHITELIST ) and autoapprove only those.

admin UI checks server-side (via /api/me ) and does not rely on client-side role

toggles.

import jwt from "jsonwebtoken"; import db from "../db.js"; import {
JWT_SECRET } from "../config.js"; export default function authCheck(req,
res, next) { const header = req.headers.authorization; if (!header) return
res.status(401).json({ error: "No token" }); const token = header.split("
")[1]; try { const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET); db.get("SELECT
* FROM users WHERE id=?", [decoded.id], (err, user) => { if (err || !user)
return res.status(401).json({ error: "Invalid token" }); req.user = user;
next(); }); } catch (e) { res.status(401).json({ error: "Invalid token"
}); } }

import rateLimit from "express-rate-limit"; export const aiLimiter =

message: { error: "Rate limit exceeded. Wait a minute." } }); export const
authLimiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 60 * 1000, max:

requests. Try again later." } });

export default function adminOnly(req, res, next) { if (req.user.role !==
"admin") return res.status(403).json({ error: "Admins only" }); next(); }

port: Number(process.env.SMTP_PORT || 587),
secure: process.env.SMTP_SECURE === 'true',
auth: {

}

function isAdminEmail(email) {
if (!email) return false;
const lower = email.toLowerCase();
if (ADMIN_EMAILS.includes(lower)) return true;
return lower.endsWith(ADMIN_DOMAIN.toLowerCase());
}

6) core/serializers.py

from rest_framework import serializers from django.contrib.auth import
get_user_model User = get_user_model() class
SignupSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer): password =
serializers.CharField(write_only=True, min_length=8) class Meta: model =
User fields = ('username','email','password','first_name','last_name') def
create(self, validated_data): password = validated_data.pop('password')
user = User(**validated_data) user.set_password(password) # role &
approved set in signals or view user.save() return user class
UserSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer): class Meta: model = User
fields =
('id','username','email','first_name','last_name','role','approved')

from django.db import models from django.conf import settings class
AuditLog(models.Model): user = models.ForeignKey(settings.AUTH_USER_MODEL,

from .models import AuditLog from django.utils import timezone import json
def audit(user, action, meta=None): meta_json = json.dumps(meta) if meta
is not None else None AuditLog.objects.create(user=user, action=action,
meta=meta_json)

# Optional: automatically log admin POST requests. Use sparingly. from
django.utils.deprecation import MiddlewareMixin from .utils.audit import
audit class AuditMiddleware(MiddlewareMixin): def process_view(self,
request, view_func, view_args, view_kwargs): # only log authenticated
actions on non-safe methods if request.user.is_authenticated and
request.method not in ('GET','HEAD','OPTIONS'): action = f"
{request.method} {request.path}" try: body = request.body.decode('utf-8')
if request.body else '' except: body = '' audit(request.user, action,
meta={"body": body}) return None

import React, {useState, useEffect} from 'react'; import { setToken } from
'../utils/auth'; export default function Login() { const [email,setEmail]
= useState(''); const [password,setPassword] = useState(''); const
[msg,setMsg] = useState(''); async function submit(e){ e.preventDefault();
const r = await fetch('/api/auth/login/', { method:'POST', headers:
{'Content-Type':'application/json'},
body:JSON.stringify({email,password})}); const j = await r.json();
if(!r.ok){ setMsg(j.detail || j.error || 'Login failed'); return; } // For
Simple JWT, server returns access & refresh setToken(j.access, j.refresh);
window.location = '/dashboard'; } // handle oauth redirect with url params
(if server redirects with tokens) useEffect(()=> { const params = new
URLSearchParams(window.location.search); const access =
params.get('access'); const refresh = params.get('refresh'); if (access &&
refresh) { setToken(access, refresh); window.history.replaceState({},'',
'/dashboard'); window.location='/dashboard'; } }, []); return ( <div
className="card"> <h2>Login</h2> <form onSubmit={submit}> <input value=
{email} onChange={e=>setEmail(e.target.value)} placeholder="Email" />
<input type="password" value={password} onChange=
{e=>setPassword(e.target.value)} placeholder="Password" />
<button>Login</button> </form> <div className="oauth"> <a
href="/accounts/google/login/?process=login">Login with Google</a> <a
href="/accounts/facebook/login/?process=login">Login with Facebook</a> <a
href="/accounts/tiktok/login/?process=login">Login with TikTok</a> </div>
<div>{msg}</div> </div> ); }

Note: allauth routes like /accounts/google/login/ will handle the redirect flow for the
web. Use process=login query param. For TikTok you may need to register a custom
provider or implement a small redirect view that starts the TikTok OAuth dance.

3) main.js
Place at /js/main.js . This adds small background particle animation, contact form
handler, and sets the copyright.
// Background canvas particles (lightweight) (() => { const canvas =
document.getElementById('bg-canvas'); if (!canvas) return; const ctx =
canvas.getContext('2d'); let w = canvas.width = innerWidth; let h =
canvas.height = innerHeight; const particles = []; const count =
Math.round(Math.max(20, Math.min(80, w / 25))); function rand(min, max){
return Math.random()*(max-min)+min; } for(let i=0;i<count;i++){
particles.push({ x: Math.random()*w, y: Math.random()*h, r: rand(0.6,
2.4), vx: rand(-0.3,0.8), vy: rand(-0.2,0.4), alpha: rand(0.05, 0.18) });
} function resize(){ w = canvas.width = innerWidth; h = canvas.height =
innerHeight; } addEventListener('resize', resize); function tick(){
ctx.clearRect(0,0,w,h); for(const p of particles){ p.x += p.vx; p.y +=
p.vy; if (p.x < -10) p.x = w+10; if (p.x > w+10) p.x = -10; if (p.y >
h+10) p.y = -10; ctx.beginPath(); ctx.fillStyle =
`rgba(6,182,212,${p.alpha})`; ctx.arc(p.x,p.y,p.r,0,Math.PI*2);
ctx.fill(); } requestAnimationFrame(tick); } tick(); })(); // contact form
submit (simple) (() => { const form =
document.getElementById('contactForm'); if (!form) return;
form.addEventListener('submit', async (e) => { e.preventDefault(); const
btn = form.querySelector('button[type="submit"]'); const msg =
document.getElementById('contactMsg'); btn.disabled = true;
msg.textContent = 'Sending...'; const data = new URLSearchParams(new
FormData(form)); try { // POST to API endpoint - change /api/contact to
your endpoint const res = await fetch('/api/contact', { method: 'POST',
body: data }); if (res.ok) { msg.textContent = 'Message sent â€” we will
reply shortly.'; form.reset(); } else { msg.textContent = 'Failed to send.
Try help@cyberkeris.com'; } } catch (err) { msg.textContent = 'Network
error. Try again later.'; } finally { btn.disabled = false; } }); })(); //
small helpers document.getElementById('year') &&
(document.getElementById('year').textContent = new Date().getFullYear());

const limiter = rateLimit({ windowMs: 60 * 1000, max: CONTACT_MAX_PER_MIN,
message: { error: 'Rate limit exceeded. Try again in a minute.' } });
router.post('/', limiter, async (req, res) => { const { name, email,
message } = req.body; if (!name || !email || !message) return
res.status(400).json({ error: 'name,email,message required' }); try {
const id = uuidv4(); // persist message (simple sqlite insert)

}); } }); module.exports = router;

5) routes/assistant.js
// routes/assistant.js const express = require('express'); const router =
express.Router(); const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit'); const {
callLLM } = require('../utils/ai_client'); const { verifyJwtOrApiKey } =
require('../utils/auth'); const db = require('../utils/db').db; const
logger = require('../utils/logger'); const ASSISTANT_MAX_PER_MIN =
Number(process.env.ASSISTANT_MAX_PER_MIN || 6); const limiter =
rateLimit({ windowMs: 60 * 1000, max: ASSISTANT_MAX_PER_MIN, message: {
error: 'Rate limit exceeded.' } }); // chat endpoint: POST
/api/assistant/chat router.post('/chat', limiter, async (req, res) => {
try { // auth: accept either JWT Bearer or ASSISTANT_API_KEY header const
auth = verifyJwtOrApiKey(req); if (!auth.authorized) return
res.status(401).json({ error: 'unauthorized' }); // messages expected:
[{role:'user', content:'...'}] or { prompt: "..." } let messages =
req.body.messages; if (!messages) { const prompt = req.body.prompt; if
(!prompt) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'messages or prompt
required' }); messages = [{ role: 'user', content: prompt }]; } // call
LLM const reply = await callLLM(messages, { userId: auth.userId || null
}); // log chat (simple DB) db.run('INSERT INTO
ai_logs(user_id,prompt,response,created_at)
VALUES(?,?,?,datetime("now"))', [auth.userId || null,
JSON.stringify(messages), reply], (err) => { if (err) logger.warn('ai log
failed', err); }); res.json({ reply }); } catch (e) {
logger.error('assistant error', e); res.status(500).json({ error:
'assistant_error' }); } }); module.exports = router;

6) utils/mailer.js
// utils/mailer.js const nodemailer = require('nodemailer'); const logger
= require('./logger'); const transporter = nodemailer.createTransport({
host: process.env.SMTP_HOST, port: Number(process.env.SMTP_PORT || 587),
secure: process.env.SMTP_SECURE === 'true', auth: { user:
process.env.SMTP_USER, pass: process.env.SMTP_PASS } }); async function
sendContactMail({ name, email, message }) { const html = `<p>
<strong>Contact message</strong></p> <p><strong>From:</strong> ${name}
&lt;${email}&gt;</p> <p>${message.replace(/\n/g,'<br/>')}</p>`; await
transporter.sendMail({ from: process.env.SMTP_FROM, to:
process.env.HELP_EMAIL, subject: `Contact from ${name} <${email}>`, html
}); } async function sendAdminNotification({ name, email, message }) {
const adminList = (process.env.ADMIN_EMAILS ||
'').split(',').map(s=>s.trim()).filter(Boolean); if (!adminList.length)
return; const text = `New contact from ${name} <${email}> â€” ${message}`;
await transporter.sendMail({ from: process.env.SMTP_FROM, to: adminList,
subject: `New contact: ${name}`, text }); } module.exports = {
sendContactMail, sendAdminNotification };

7) utils/ai_client.js
// utils/ai_client.js - simple OpenAI-compatible client using global fetch
(Node 18+) const OPENAI_API_KEY = process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY; const
OPENAI_API_URL = process.env.OPENAI_API_URL ||
'https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions'; const OPENAI_MODEL =
process.env.OPENAI_MODEL || 'gpt-4o-mini'; async function
callLLM(messages, opts = {}) { const payload = { model: OPENAI_MODEL,
messages, max_tokens: 800, temperature: 0.2 }; const res = await
fetch(OPENAI_API_URL, { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type':
'application/json', 'Authorization': `Bearer ${OPENAI_API_KEY}` }, body:
JSON.stringify(payload) }); if (!res.ok) { const t = await res.text();
throw new Error(`LLM error ${res.status}: ${t}`); } const jr = await
res.json(); // support both chat and text responses const assistantText =
jr.choices && jr.choices[0] && (jr.choices[0].message?.content ||
jr.choices[0].text) || ''; return assistantText; } module.exports = {
callLLM };

// utils/auth.js - check JWT or API key const jwt =
require('jsonwebtoken'); function verifyJwtOrApiKey(req) { // API key
header const apiKey = req.headers['x-api-key'] || req.query.api_key; if
(apiKey && process.env.ASSISTANT_API_KEY && apiKey ===
process.env.ASSISTANT_API_KEY) { return { authorized: true, method:
'api_key', userId: null }; } // bearer jwt const h =
req.headers.authorization; if (!h) return { authorized: false }; const
token = h.split(' ')[1]; if (!token) return { authorized: false }; try {
const data = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET); return {
authorized: true, method: 'jwt', userId: data.id || data.userId || null,
claims: data }; } catch (e) { return { authorized: false }; } }
module.exports = { verifyJwtOrApiKey };

9) utils/db.js (sqlite init)
// utils/db.js const sqlite3 = require('sqlite3').verbose(); const path =
require('path'); const fs = require('fs'); const logger =
require('./logger'); let db; async function initDb(dbPath) { const p =
dbPath || path.join(__dirname, '..', 'data', 'cyberkeris.db'); const dir =
path.dirname(p); if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) fs.mkdirSync(dir, { recursive:
true }); db = new sqlite3.Database(p); // create tables if not exist
db.serialize(() => { db.run(`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS contacts (id TEXT
PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT, email TEXT, message TEXT, created_at DATETIME)`);
db.run(`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ai_logs (id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY
AUTOINCREMENT, user_id TEXT, prompt TEXT, response TEXT, created_at
DATETIME)`); }); logger.info('DB initialized at ' + p); } module.exports =
{ initDb, get db() { return db; } };

const winston = require('winston'); const logger = winston.createLogger({
level: 'info', format: winston.format.combine( winston.format.timestamp(),
winston.format.printf(({ timestamp, level, message }) => `${timestamp}
[${level}] ${message}`) ), transports: [ new winston.transports.Console()
] }); module.exports = logger;

4. npm install
5. node server.js (or npm start ) â€” server will listen on PORT .

be {ok:true} and email delivered to help@cyberkeris.com .
7. Test assistant (two ways):

POST /api/assistant/chat
Headers: x-api-key: <ASSISTANT_API_KEY>
Body: { "prompt": "Summarize the current project status" }

With JWT (if you already have user JWT from your auth system): Authorization:
Bearer <token> and body either {"prompt":"..."} or {"messages":
[{role:'user',content:'...'}]} .

8. Add Nginx config and obtain SSL (Certbot) or use Cloudflare origin certs, then
proxy /api/ to http://127.0.0.1:3000/api/ .

Security & production notes (must-read)
SMTP: Use a reliable SMTP provider (SendGrid, Mailgun, Amazon SES). Add SPF &
DKIM records for cyberkeris.com immediately.
OpenAI Key: Keep OPENAI_API_KEY secret and rotate periodically. Monitor usage to
avoid unexpected bills.
Rate limits: Default is conservative.
Tune CONTACT_MAX_PER_MIN and ASSISTANT_MAX_PER_MIN to your traffic profile.
Authentication: I provided flexible assistant auth (JWT or ASSISTANT_API_KEY). For
public UI, prefer JWT from your main auth system. Use ASSISTANT_API_KEY only for
server-to-server or admin scripts.
Logging & storage: Audit logs are stored in ai_logs + contacts . Backup
the data/ folder regularly and secure it (permissions).
Harden Nginx: enable HSTS, set ssl_protocols TLSv1.2 TLSv1.3 , and tune security
headers.

# CyberKeris â€” Website + Assistant This repo contains the public website
and AI assistant UI for CyberKeris Technologies, plus a Node/Express
backend (in a separate backend folder) that exposes: - `/api/contact` â€”
contact form POST - `/api/assistant/chat` â€” assistant chat endpoint (POST
{ prompt } or { messages }) - `/api/auth/*` â€” auth endpoints
(login/signup) if present ## Quick start (frontend) 1. Place `/public`
files on your webserver root (e.g. `/var/www/cyberkeris/public`) 2. Ensure
backend is reachable at `/api/` (Nginx proxy to Node app) 3. Update logo
at `/assets/cyberkeris_logo.png`

7) How to wire to your backend (quick checklist)

149/180

12/7/25, 12:46 PM

Create website for cyberkeris

1. Place these frontend files under your web root (e.g. /var/www/cyberkeris/public ),
ensure /assets/cyberkeris_logo.png exists (replace filename accordingly).
2. Backend must be accessible as /api/ (Nginx config in previous step
proxies /api/ to http://127.0.0.1:3000/api/ ).
3. For login/signup the pages POST to /api/auth/login/ and /api/auth/signup/ . If
your auth endpoint differs, update the fetch URLs.

#!/bin/bash set -e # CyberKeris VPS provision script (Ubuntu/Debian) #
Usage: sudo bash provision.sh yourdomain.com admin@example.com DOMAIN="$1"
EMAIL="$2" if [ -z "$DOMAIN" ]; then echo "Usage: sudo bash provision.sh
yourdomain.com admin@example.com" exit 1 fi if [ -z "$EMAIL" ]; then
EMAIL="admin@${DOMAIN}" fi APP_DIR="/var/www/cyberkeris"
BACKEND_DIR="${APP_DIR}/backend" PUBLIC_DIR="${APP_DIR}/public" echo "[*]
Updating system..." apt update && apt upgrade -y echo "[*] Install deps:
nginx, git, curl, build-essential, unzip" apt install -y nginx git curl
build-essential unzip echo "[*] Install Node.js 18.x and PM2" curl -fsSL
https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_18.x | bash - apt install -y nodejs npm
install -g pm2 echo "[*] Create application dirs" mkdir -p
"${BACKEND_DIR}" mkdir -p "${PUBLIC_DIR}" chown -R $USER:$USER
"${APP_DIR}" cat > /etc/nginx/sites-available/cyberkeris <<'NGCONF' server
{ listen 80; server_name __DOMAIN_PLACEHOLDER__
www.__DOMAIN_PLACEHOLDER__; root __APP_ROOT__/public; index index.html;
location /api/ { proxy_pass http://127.0.0.1:3000/api/; proxy_set_header
Host $host; proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme; proxy_set_header X-Real-IP
$remote_addr; proxy_http_version 1.1; proxy_set_header Connection ""; }
location / { try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html; } } NGCONF # Replace
placeholders sed -i "s|__DOMAIN_PLACEHOLDER__|${DOMAIN}|g"
/etc/nginx/sites-available/cyberkeris sed -i "s|__APP_ROOT__|${APP_DIR}|g"
/etc/nginx/sites-available/cyberkeris ln -sf /etc/nginx/sitesavailable/cyberkeris /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/cyberkeris nginx -t &&
systemctl reload nginx echo "[*] Install Certbot and try to issue an SSL
cert" apt install -y certbot python3-certbot-nginx if certbot --nginx -d
"${DOMAIN}" -d "www.${DOMAIN}" --non-interactive --agree-tos -m
"${EMAIL}"; then echo "[*] Certificate installed" else echo "[!] Certbot
failed. Ensure DNS for ${DOMAIN} points to this server and run certbot
manually." fi echo "Provision finished. - Upload your site files to
${PUBLIC_DIR} - Upload backend zip to ${BACKEND_DIR} and unzip - Configure
backend .env then run: cd ${BACKEND_DIR} npm install pm2 start
ecosystem.config.js --only cyberkeris - After pm2 start, check: curl -I
http://127.0.0.1:3000/health "

3) JWT integration snippet â€” utils/auth.js (use this
version to support common token shapes)
Replace your utils/auth.js content with:
// utils/auth.js - flexible JWT / API key verifier const jwt =
require('jsonwebtoken'); function verifyJwtOrApiKey(req) { // check for
server-to-server API key first const apiKey = req.headers['x-api-key'] ||
req.query.api_key; if (apiKey && process.env.ASSISTANT_API_KEY && apiKey
=== process.env.ASSISTANT_API_KEY) { return { authorized: true, method:
'api_key', userId: null, claims: null }; } // Bearer token const
authHeader = req.headers.authorization || ''; const parts =
authHeader.split(' '); if (parts.length !== 2 || parts[0] !== 'Bearer')
return { authorized: false }; const token = parts[1]; try { // If you use
an external JWKS/OIDC provider, replace jwt.verify with appropriate
verification const claims = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET); //
common claim shapes: sub, id, userId const userId = claims.sub ||
claims.id || claims.userId || null; return { authorized: true, method:
'jwt', userId, claims }; } catch (err) { // token invalid or expired
return { authorized: false }; } } module.exports = { verifyJwtOrApiKey };

If you use OIDC/JWKS: use the jwks-rsa library and verify tokens against the public
signing keys from your identity provider â€” I can generate that wiring if you tell me the
OIDC issuer.

/backend/utils/auth.js (JWT + API key)
import jwt from "jsonwebtoken"; export function verifyJwtOrApiKey(req) {
// server-to-server API key const apiKey = req.headers["x-api-key"]; if
(apiKey && apiKey === process.env.ASSISTANT_API_KEY) { return { ok: true,
userId: "system", method: "api-key" }; } // Bearer JWT const header =
req.headers.authorization || ""; const [type, token] = header.split(" ");
if (type !== "Bearer" || !token) { return { ok: false }; } try { const
claims = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET); const userId =
claims.sub || claims.id || claims.userId; return { ok: true, userId,
claims }; } catch (e) { return { ok: false }; } }

import nodemailer from "nodemailer"; import dotenv from "dotenv";

process.env.SMTP_HOST, port: Number(process.env.SMTP_PORT), secure:

/backend/routes/assistant.js
import express from "express"; import { OpenAI } from "openai"; import {
verifyJwtOrApiKey } from "../utils/auth.js"; const router =
express.Router(); const client = new OpenAI({ apiKey:
process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY }); router.post("/chat", async (req, res) => {
const auth = verifyJwtOrApiKey(req); if (!auth.ok) return
res.status(401).json({ error: "Unauthorized" }); const { prompt } =
req.body; try { const ai = await client.chat.completions.create({ model:
process.env.OPENAI_MODEL, messages: [ { role: "system", content: "You are
CyberKeris AI Assistant." }, { role: "user", content: prompt } ] });
res.json({ reply: ai.choices?.[0]?.message?.content || "No response" }); }
catch (err) { res.json({ error: err.message }); } }); export default
router;

2 â€” BACKEND ADDITIONS (copy into backend/ )
These patches plug into the existing Node backend you already have. I assume the code
base created earlier (server.js, routes folder, utils). Add/replace the following files.
Important: You already have routes/contact.js and routes/assistant.js . Below I
provide new routes/auth.js , routes/progress.js , DB schema for refresh tokens and
projects, and updated utils/auth.js that includes refresh token verify and JWT

2.1 backend/routes/auth.js
// routes/auth.js (CommonJS style if your server is CommonJS; adapt
`import`/`export` as needed) const express = require('express'); const jwt
= require('jsonwebtoken'); const bcrypt = require('bcryptjs'); const { v4:
uuidv4 } = require('uuid'); const db = require('../utils/db').db; const
router = express.Router(); // Signup -> create user (approved: false by
default) router.post('/signup', async (req, res) => { const { email,
password, first_name } = req.body; if (!email || !password) return
res.status(400).json({ error: 'missing' }); const hashed = await
bcrypt.hash(password, 10); const id = uuidv4(); db.run('INSERT INTO
users(id,email,first_name,password,approved,role,created_at)
VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,?,datetime("now"))', [id, email.toLowerCase(), first_name
|| '', hashed, 0, 'user'], (err) => { if (err) return
res.status(500).json({ error: 'db' }); // notify admins via mailer
(optional) res.json({ ok: true, id, status: 'pending_approval' }); }); });
// Login -> returns access + refresh tokens (store refresh in DB)
router.post('/login', (req, res) => { const { email, password } =
req.body; db.get('SELECT * FROM users WHERE email = ?',
[email.toLowerCase()], async (err, user) => { if (err || !user) return
res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid' }); if (!user.approved) return
res.status(403).json({ error: 'pending' }); const ok = await
bcrypt.compare(password, user.password); if (!ok) return
res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid' }); const access = jwt.sign({ id:
user.id, email: user.email, role: user.role }, process.env.JWT_SECRET, {
expiresIn: '15m' }); const refresh = jwt.sign({ id: user.id },
process.env.JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn: '30d' }); const tokenId = uuidv4();
db.run('INSERT INTO refresh_tokens(id,user_id,token,created_at)
VALUES(?,?,?,datetime("now"))', [tokenId, user.id, refresh], (e) => { if
(e) console.error(e); }); res.json({ access, refresh }); }); }); //
Refresh endpoint router.post('/refresh', (req, res) => { const { refresh }
= req.body; if (!refresh) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'missing'
}); // verify token exists in db db.get('SELECT * FROM refresh_tokens
WHERE token = ?', [refresh], (err, row) => { if (err || !row) return

3 â€” DATABASE SCHEMA (SQLite)
Save as backend/schema.sql and run once (or let the server init create tables). This
schema includes users, refresh_tokens, projects, milestones, audit_logs, contacts, ai_logs.
BEGIN TRANSACTION; CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users ( id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
email TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL, first_name TEXT, password TEXT NOT NULL, role
TEXT DEFAULT 'user', approved INTEGER DEFAULT 0, created_at DATETIME
DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ); CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS refresh_tokens (
id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, user_id TEXT, token TEXT, created_at DATETIME DEFAULT
CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE
CASCADE ); CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS projects ( id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, name
TEXT, description TEXT, owner_id TEXT, status TEXT, progress INTEGER
DEFAULT 0, created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ); CREATE TABLE
IF NOT EXISTS milestones ( id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, project_id TEXT, title
TEXT, description TEXT, due_date DATETIME, status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending',
created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP, FOREIGN KEY(project_id)
REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE ); CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS
audit_logs ( id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, user_id TEXT, action
TEXT, meta TEXT, created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ); CREATE
TABLE IF NOT EXISTS contacts ( id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT, email TEXT,
message TEXT, created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ); CREATE
TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ai_logs ( id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
user_id TEXT, prompt TEXT, response TEXT, created_at DATETIME DEFAULT
CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ); COMMIT;

4.1 backend/oauth.js (example wiring)
const passport = require('passport'); const GoogleStrategy =
require('passport-google-oauth20').Strategy; const FacebookStrategy =
require('passport-facebook').Strategy; const db =
require('./utils/db').db; passport.serializeUser((user, done) =>
done(null, user.id)); passport.deserializeUser((id, done) => {
db.get('SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = ?', [id], (err, row) => done(err,
row)); }); passport.use(new GoogleStrategy({ clientID:
process.env.SOCIAL_GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID, clientSecret:
process.env.SOCIAL_GOOGLE_SECRET, callbackURL: process.env.BASE_URL +
'/api/auth/oauth/google/callback' }, (accessToken, refreshToken, profile,
done) => { const email = (profile.emails && profile.emails[0] &&
profile.emails[0].value) || null; // Upsert user by email db.get('SELECT *
FROM users WHERE email = ?', [email], (err, user) => { if (user) return
done(null, user); const id = require('uuid').v4(); db.run('INSERT INTO
users(id,email,first_name,approved,role,created_at)
VALUES(?,?,?,?,?,datetime("now"))', [id, email, profile.name.givenName ||
'', 0, 'user'], (e) => { db.get('SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = ?', [id],
(er, u2) => done(er, u2)); }); }); })); // Facebook is analogous
module.exports = passport;

4.2 Routes to start OAuth
Add /api/auth/oauth/google (passport.authenticate('google', { scope: ['email','profile'] }))
and callback /api/auth/oauth/google/callback which creates user and then either issues
tokens or redirects to frontend with a one-time code that exchanges for JWT (see earlier
"convert-token" flow).

TikTok
TikTok provider is not in Passport core. Use their OAuth endpoints (server-side) and
exchange the code for user info, then upsert user similarly. If you want, I can generate a
full TikTok provider module â€” say "TikTok please" and I'll produce it.

Upload the zip to VPS:

Then run sudo bash provision.sh yourdomain.com admin@yourdomain.com (the script will
configure nginx & try to request certificates via certbot).
